<tr class="sortbottom" style="text-align:left;">
<td colspan="6" style="width:1px;"><b>Notes</b><br/><div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: lower-alpha;">
<div class="mw-references-wrap mw-references-columns"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Countries and territories, and two international conveyances where cases were diagnosed. Nationality and location of original infection may vary. In some countries, the cases cover several territories, as noted accordingly.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-ccc-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-ccc_3-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Cumulative confirmed cases reported to date. The actual number of infections and cases are likely to be higher than reported.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[1]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Total deaths may not necessarily add up due to the frequency of values updating for each individual location.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-5">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Reported recoveries. May not correspond to actual current figures and not all recoveries may be reported. Total recoveries may not necessarily add up due to the frequency of values updating for each individual location.<br/>"–" denotes that no reliable or up-to-date data is currently available for that territory, not that the value is zero.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-11">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>United States</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>Figures include cases identified on the <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_on_cruise_ships#Grand_Princess" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic on cruise ships"><i>Grand Princess</i></a>.</li><li>Data is from unofficial trackers and not from the official <a href="/wiki/Centers_for_Disease_Control_and_Prevention" title="Centers for Disease Control and Prevention">Centers for Disease Control and Prevention</a> (CDC).</li><li>Figures from the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">United States Department of Defense</a> are only released on a branch-by branch basis since April 2020, without distinction between domestic and foreign deployment, and cases may be reported to local health authorities.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DoD_stop_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-DoD_stop-7">[3]</a></sup></li><li>Figures from the Department of Defense are as follows:<div><ul>
<li>The DoD reports a total of <b>1,752</b> cases, <b>6</b> deaths, and <b>98</b> recovered.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">Navy</a> reports <b>514</b> cases, <b>1</b> deaths, and <b>26</b> recovered.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-US_Navy_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-US_Navy-9">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">Air Force</a> reports <b>465</b> cases, <b>0</b> deaths, and <b>39</b> recovered.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[6]</a></sup></li>
</ul></div></li><li>Cases for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_on_aircraft_carriers" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic on aircraft carriers">USS <i>Theodore Roosevelt</i></a>, currently docked at Guam, are reported separate from national figures, but included in the Navy's totals.</li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-15"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-15">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Spain</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>Including the autonomous cities of <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_Ceuta" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in Ceuta">Ceuta</a> and <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_Melilla" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in Melilla">Melilla</a>.</li><li>Testing has been restricted to at-risk people showing symptoms.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[9]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-19"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-19">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Italy</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Only at-risk people showing symptoms have been tested from 27 February 2020 and onwards.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[12]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-22"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-22">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Germany</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Not all state authorities count recoveries.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-zeit_21-0"><a href="#cite_note-zeit-21">[14]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-24"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-24">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>China</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>Excluding 1,268 <a href="/wiki/Asymptomatic" title="Asymptomatic">asymptomatic</a> cases under medical observation as of 4 April 2020<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=2019%E2%80%9320_coronavirus_pandemic_by_country_and_territory&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup></li><li>Asymptomatic cases were not reported prior to 31 March 2020.</li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-29"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-29">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>France</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>Testing has been restricted to at-risk people showing severe symptoms.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[17]</a></sup></li><li>Excluding all <a href="/wiki/Overseas_department_and_region" title="Overseas department and region">Overseas departments and regions</a> and <a href="/wiki/Overseas_collectivity" title="Overseas collectivity">Overseas collectivities</a>.</li><li>Recoveries only include hospitalised cases.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gouvernement.fr_27-0"><a href="#cite_note-gouvernement.fr-27">[18]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-France_Geodes_28-0"><a href="#cite_note-France_Geodes-28">[19]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-31"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-31">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Iran</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Due to a shortage of resources, testing is restricted to only severe cases.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[20]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-34"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-34">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>United Kingdom</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>Excluding all <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_British_Overseas_Territories" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in British Overseas Territories">British Overseas Territories</a> and Crown dependencies.</li><li>As of 23 March 2020, the United Kingdom government does not publish the number of recoveries. Last update on 22 March reported 135 recovered patients.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[22]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-42"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-42">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Netherlands</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>All four constituent countries of the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Kingdom of the Netherlands</a> (i.e. the country - as opposed to the Kingdom - of the Netherlands - in this table row -, Aruba, Curaçao and Sint Maarten) are listed separately.</li><li><a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Netherlands" title="Caribbean Netherlands">Special municipalities</a> are listed separately.</li><li>The Dutch Government agency RIVM, responsible for the constituent country the Netherlands, does not count its number of recoveries<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[29]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-52"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-52">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Sweden</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Testing of suspected infections has been cut back in the whole country in the period around 12 March 2020, in order to focus efforts on people with increased risk of serious illness and complications.</li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-57"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-57">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Norway</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>From 13 March 2020, testing of the normal population was discontinued, and is now only reserved for health professionals and acutely ill people in vulnerable groups.</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_Institute_of_Public_Health" title="Norwegian Institute of Public Health">Norwegian Institute of Public Health</a> states that there are more infected people in Norway than the figures show. The dark figures are presumed to be higher because of limited testing.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-VG_54-0"><a href="#cite_note-VG-54">[40]</a></sup></li><li>Estimation of number of coronavirus infected:<div><ul>
<li>As of 23 March 2020, according to figures from just over 40% of all GPs in Norway, <b>20,200</b> patients have been registered with the "corona code" R991. The figure includes both cases where the patient has been diagnosed with coronavirus infection through testing, and where the GP has used the "corona code" after assessing the patient's symptoms against the criteria by the Norwegian Institute of Public Health.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[41]</a></sup></li>
<li>As of 24 March 2020, the Norwegian Institute of Public Health estimates that between <b>7,120</b> and <b>23,140</b> Norwegians are infected with the coronavirus.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56">[42]</a></sup></li>
</ul></div></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-58"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-58">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Australia</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Excluding the cases from <i><a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_on_cruise_ships#Diamond_Princess" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic on cruise ships">Diamond Princess</a></i> cruise ship which are classified as "on an international conveyance". Ten cases, including one fatality recorded by the Australian government.</li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-63"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-63">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Russia</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>Including cases from the <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_Crimea" title="Political status of Crimea">disputed</a> <a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_Crimea" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in Crimea">Crimea</a>, which was <a href="/wiki/Annexation_of_Crimea_by_the_Russian_Federation" title="Annexation of Crimea by the Russian Federation">annexed by Russia</a> in 2014 but remains internationally recognized as being under <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukrainian</a> sovereignty.</li><li>Excluding the cases from <i><a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_on_cruise_ships#Diamond_Princess" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic on cruise ships">Diamond Princess</a></i> cruise ship which are classified as "on an international conveyance".</li><li>One fatality was not officially recorded by the Russian authorities as caused by coronavirus.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60"><a href="#cite_note-60">[44]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61"><a href="#cite_note-61">[45]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[46]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-70"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-70">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Denmark</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>The autonomous territories of the <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_the_Faroe_Islands" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in the Faroe Islands">Faroe Islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_Greenland" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in Greenland">Greenland</a> are listed separately.</li><li>From 12 March to 1 April 2020, testing primarily focussed on people with more serious symptoms, vulnerable people and health professionals. Before and after this period testing was done more broadly, among others including people with mild symptoms and people that have been in close contact with an infected person.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69"><a href="#cite_note-69">[52]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-89"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-89">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Finland</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>Excluding the autonomous region of the <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_the_%C3%85land_Islands" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in the Åland Islands">Åland Islands</a>.</li><li>Not all suspected infections are tested. As of 31 March 2020, testing focuses on at-risk people and patients with severe symptoms of respiratory tract infection, as well as healthcare and social welfare personnel.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86"><a href="#cite_note-86">[68]</a></sup> Specimens from mildly symptomatic and returning travellers can still be taken at the discretion of the treating physician.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87"><a href="#cite_note-87">[69]</a></sup></li><li>There is no reliable or frequently published national data source which provides counts of recoveries. However, as of 1 April 2020, there have been hundreds of recoveries. The exact number is not known, as only a small proportion of patients have been hospitalized.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88"><a href="#cite_note-88">[70]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-93"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-93">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Serbia</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Excluding <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_Kosovo" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in Kosovo">Kosovo</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92"><a href="#cite_note-92">[73]</a></sup></li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-112"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-112">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Ukraine</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Excluding cases from the <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_Crimea" title="Political status of Crimea">disputed</a> <a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_Crimea" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in Crimea">Crimea</a>, which was <a href="/wiki/Annexation_of_Crimea_by_the_Russian_Federation" title="Annexation of Crimea by the Russian Federation">annexed by Russia</a> in 2014 but remains internationally recognized as being under <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukrainian</a> sovereignty. Because the Russian authorities are tabulating cases from Crimea, they are included in the Russian total. Also excluding cases from the unrecognized <a href="/wiki/Donetsk_People%27s_Republic" title="Donetsk People's Republic">Donetsk</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luhansk_People%27s_Republic" title="Luhansk People's Republic">Lugansk</a> People's Republics.</li></ol></div></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-115"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-115">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Egypt</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Includes cases identified on the <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_on_cruise_ships#MS_River_Anuket" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic on cruise ships">MS <i>River Anuket</i></a>.</li></ol></div></span>

<li id="cite_note-119"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-119">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Morocco</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Including cases in Western Sahara territory controlled by Morocco. <li id="cite_note-129"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-129">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><i><b>Diamond Princess</b></i><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>The British cruise ship <i><a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_on_cruise_ships#Diamond_Princess" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic on cruise ships">Diamond Princess</a></i> was in Japanese waters, and Japanese administration was asked to manage its quarantine, with the passengers having not entered Japan. Therefore, this case is neither included in the Japanese government's official count nor in United Kingdom's one. The World Health Organization classifies the cases as being located "on an international conveyance".</li></ol></div></span>

<li id="cite_note-147"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-147">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Cyprus</b><div><ol style="list-style-type:none"><li>Excluding <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_Akrotiri_and_Dhekelia" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in Akrotiri and Dhekelia">Akrotiri and Dhekelia</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Self-declared_states" title="Self-declared states"><i>de facto state</i></a> of <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_in_Northern_Cyprus" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic in Northern Cyprus">Northern Cyprus</a>.</li></ol></div></span>

<li id="cite_note-255"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-255">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>MS <i>Zaandam</i></b> and <b>MS <i>Rotterdam</i></b><div><ol style="list-style-type:decimal"><li>The cruise ship <a href="/wiki/2020_coronavirus_pandemic_on_cruise_ships#Zaandam" title="2020 coronavirus pandemic on cruise ships">MS <i>Zaandam</i></a> became stranded off the coast of Chile after being denied entry to ports since 14 March 2020.</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/MS_Rotterdam" title="MS Rotterdam">MS <i>Rotterdam</i></a> rendezvoused with the <i>Zaandam</i> on March 26 off the coast of Panama City to provide support and evacuate healthy passengers. Both transited the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Panama_canal" title="Panama canal">Panama canal</a>, and have now docked in Florida.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-254"><a href="#cite_note-254">[222]</a></sup></li><li>MS <i>Zaandam</i> and <i>Rotterdam</i>'s numbers are currently not counted in any national figures.</li></ol></div></span>
